name:h‍a‍n‍n‍a‍h‍_‍h‍u‍a‍n‍g‍_‍5
info:Guestroom (Double bed)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:It was almost 2pm when a group of four people arrived at the magnificent lobby on the sixth floor of the hotel. There were three hotel employees standing at the front desk, which was empty and no passengers were checking in.
We found a tall, handsome young man to check in. The young man received us with a standard etiquette:
I asked: "Is it possible to upgrade the room? I didn't get the suite package of the same price."
The young man replied: "You are already an executive room, you can't upgrade."
I was frustrated but didn't give up and asked: "Is there a south-facing room?"
The answer was "The south-facing room has not been cleaned yet, you have to wait."
Question: "How long will it take?"
The answer was: "One hour",
The four relatives who went with me agreed that they didn't want to wait, so they took the north-facing room.
The front desk guy asked me for a deposit of 1,000 yuan.
He opened two adjacent rooms on the top floor, the 17th floor, and handed me the room card while speaking very quickly: "Your room is on the 17th floor, No. xx. Each room has two breakfasts every day." 
I was stunned and thought that the package did not include welcome fruit and free mini-bar refrigerators on the first day. Looking at the cold face of the front desk clerk, I was embarrassed to bother him again, so I took the room key and went upstairs.
Although I didn't get the room I wanted, I was excited when I opened the door of the room. The room was spacious and bright, clean and tidy, without a trace of dust. After all, it was a five-star hotel. The full set of sanitary ware was ROCA, and the toiletries were Seven Plus. The bathtub was the highlight of the whole room, occupying the center of the room. The open bathroom was very romantic and sentimental. If you don't want to use the open bathroom, you can also use the elegant Japanese sliding door next to it to separate the entire bathroom and bedroom. It's so convenient.
I felt a little thirsty. Seeing that the market price of drinks and snacks in the refrigerator was 140 yuan, I didn't dare to eat. I asked the front desk again to confirm that our package included refrigerator drinks before I started drinking.
After a while, we received the welcome fruit sent by the waiter. After resting in the comfortable hotel room, we started our two-night tour of Hangzhou.
The next day, we went to the restaurant for a buffet breakfast. The buffet breakfast had a wide variety of dishes, including Chinese food, Western food, sushi rolls, noodles and wontons with skin strings and scallion stew.
It is said that to see whether a five-star hotel is good or not, you have to see how good their pastries are. I specifically selected croissants, waffles, small breads, donuts (with jam fillings) and many other small pastries to try. Each one was full of butter flavor, fragrant, crispy and sweet. It was so delicious that I couldn't stop eating. It was indeed a professional, standard and high-end five-star hotel.
The hotel restaurant service was timely. I saw the hotel waiters adding dishes to the dishes quickly. If there were dishes that were almost empty, the waiters would replenish them in time. There were also many waitresses who kept cleaning up the dirty dishes that tourists had eaten and wiping the tables and chairs. . Busy all the time. It can be seen that the hotel management is in place.
After breakfast, I went outside the hotel lobby: lush greenery, blooming flowers, pavilions, fountains and waterfalls, fresh air, and a charming sky garden for a stroll. . .
The next day, I had delicious wontons for breakfast, made a bowl of tofu brain, and ate Hangzhou snacks such as skin skewers, scallion stew, and pig's trotter noodles. I was full again. . .
It was raining outside and I couldn't go out, so I went to the sky garden to enjoy the rain and listen to the sound of rain. It was very pleasant. .
Back to the room, the waitress brought welcome fruit again, haha ​​😄 said welcome once, and was welcomed again. The empty refrigerator was also filled.
There is a circus a hundred meters away from the hotel. There is a circus performance in the square outside the circus at night, which attracts many children to pull their parents to stop and watch.
There is a large Xintiandi Plaza shopping center three or four hundred meters away from the hotel, with the top 10 restaurants in Hangzhou in the center. There is also a newly opened Lianhua Supermarket, and there are subway stations on Lines 3 and 4 below, which is very convenient for eating, drinking and playing.
On the third day, we checked out at the hotel lobby, returned the key card and checked out in seconds. The deposit was also returned in seconds. .
The family of four agreed that this three-day trip to this five-star hotel was worth it. If their hotel had a package, they would try their best to grab it.

msg:Although it is not in the center of Hangzhou, the transportation is still very convenient. There are subway stations No. 3 and No. 4 nearby. It only takes half an hour to get to Hangzhou East Station. There are two large shopping malls, Xintiandi Shopping Center and Yintai Shopping Center, and a large street green park next to Hangzhou E-sports Center. There is also the Manner Coffee we love to drink, haha, the facilities are really good~
This time, I got the room voucher for his elegant partition suite, which is very cost-effective. I stayed for two nights. This suite is a compact open-plan suite. The flexible partition makes the movement line in the house full of fun. Although the area is not large, we quite like this design. The breakfast is also rich, and the vegetable and meat wontons are delicious.
However, there are still some things I want to complain about. First, our room on the 10th floor looks out to the bare large platform of the shopping mall next to it, and the view is really bad; second, the hotel breakfast ends at 10 o'clock on weekdays and is postponed to 10:30 on weekends. However, when we checked in on the first day of Qingming Festival and it was not on the weekend, it still ended at 10 o'clock. Holidays are not consistent with the weekend policy. I don’t quite understand such a rule. It is not very friendly to late risers. . .

msg:前幾日前往杭州看演出，然後就訂了這家酒店。
前台經理很好，幫我免費升級了房間。
酒店地理位置也很好，距離太陽劇場三百米。附近一百米也有一個核酸點。
點外賣很方便，也不用擔心外賣會丟。因為外賣存放的地方是行李寄存的前台桌，有監控，可以追溯，很安心。
因為行程太匆忙，沒有去吃早餐，哈哈哈。
如果下次還去看太陽劇場的演出，我還是挺願意住這家酒店的。

既然問我介意嗎 我當然介意 畢竟第二天我要開視頻會議三個小時 當我表達了介意的時候 前台女生説 “那您就取消這個訂單吧”  本人瞬間被她這樣的回覆方式堵住了一口氣 （邊上另一位入住客人也表示 怎麼可以這樣説話 還是雷迪森呢）你問我介意不介意 我當然如實回答 我大老遠跑過來 你和我説 我介意 你就取消訂單 這是星級酒店的服務水平？ 

怎麼説呢 這個酒店掛名雷迪森 但是應該是挺缺乏成熟優質的五星級國際品牌的工作人員的 也挺缺乏培訓的 整個入住碰到的工作人員 都非常冷漠 並沒有賓至如歸的感受 服務都還不如連鎖經濟酒店品牌的水平 

最後退房的時候 前台佔了兩位工作人員 我走到了左邊辦理退房 左邊的工作人員明明空着 她一定要我去右邊辦理 這都不什麼事 也並不給我帶來任何不便 但是你不能因為要方便你自己 而讓我去別的地方辦理 總而言之 感受挺差

msg:本來寄望還是高的，應該是附近的最豪華酒店之一，但是槽點不少，主要是服務跟不上價格：1到達時間是1430，要求checkin，説房間沒有打掃好。我説沒有關係，我把行李寄存，您給我門卡，我出去吃飯，吃完回來直接上房間（前台在6樓），前台一定説不行，要麼您坐着等一會，折騰半天最後找了應該是大堂領班，還重申這是酒店規定-這個絕對減分。2晚上叫了外賣，酒店説衹能放一樓，可以讓服務員送上來，然而，外賣來時電話客房服務部，無人接聽-自己下去拿完全沒問題，但是承諾的做不到居然還有客房服務部無人值守之時（8pm前），再次減分。3早上早餐還是挺豐富的，但是隨處可見未及時清理的桌面，減分。4前台checkout之時要求通知禮賓部幫助叫車，前台説您下去1樓直接叫禮賓部幫叫吧，下去一樓禮賓部直接説我們叫車系統壞了，然後速度離開，是不是也該減分？酒店旁邊感覺還是相對荒蕪，商場店也未開足人氣也無，閨女也説，居然是個如此不好玩的地方。。。疫情原因很久未出差，卻未曾想酒店服務可以如此水準下降。。。衹評價它的服務是不是配得上它的價格，以上。
